# ION Production Encyclopedia v2.3 — Conversational Receipts and Live Repair Protocol Draft

**Section path:** `30_v42_conversational_receipts_live_repair_protocol_draft_v2_3/ION_Production_Encyclopedia_v2_3_CONVERSATIONAL_RECEIPTS_AND_LIVE_REPAIR_PROTOCOL_DRAFT.md`  
**Date:** 2026-04-26  
**Authority posture:** encyclopedia protocol draft; non-production; non-runtime-mutating  
**Live root being evolved:** ION Production Encyclopedia packet, currently v2.2 LIVE V41/V42 seed  
**Live project evidence referenced:** `ION_MASTER_CURRENT_3_V41_FRONT_STAGE_COUNCIL_RUNTIME_RECEIPTS_FULL_PROJECT_20260425.zip`  
**Production claim:** false  
**Implementation claim:** false  
**Project-root mutation claim:** false

---

## 1. Protocol Receipt

```yaml
receipt_id: ion-encyclopedia-v2-3-v42-conversational-receipts-live-repair-protocol-draft-20260426
receipt_class: encyclopedia_protocol_draft
target_branch: V42_CONVERSATIONAL_RECEIPTS_AND_LIVE_REPAIR
source_basis:
  - v2_2_live_v41_v42_seed
  - v41_front_stage_council_runtime_receipts
  - v40_maintained_work_surface_and_persona_system
purpose:
  - convert the V42 seed into a dedicated protocol chapter
  - define conversational repair as an ION continuity event
  - preserve user corrections as governed state instead of ephemeral chat noise
  - specify repair classes, receipt fields, state transitions, and test targets
non_claims:
  - does not implement V42 in the ION project tree
  - does not grant production authority
  - does not override V41 claim-emission receipts
  - does not activate unrestricted agents or visual automation
  - does not claim full-suite test verification
```

---

## 2. Why V42 Exists

V41 gives ION a runtime receipt object for **front-stage claim emission**. It can classify a proposed user-facing claim into C0 through C5, bind the claim to Persona state, Relay grounding, Steward/VZ verdict, risk, emission permission, visibility, and repair obligation. That is a major step, but it governs the moment before or during emission.

V42 must govern what happens **after** emission, when live conversation reveals that a claim, target, artifact, scope, confidence level, or authority surface was wrong or incomplete.

A normal assistant treats correction as conversational embarrassment. ION treats correction as state.

The central V42 rule is:

```text
A correction is not merely an apology. A correction is a continuity event.
```

This matters because the most dangerous failures in long-horizon AI work are rarely single-message errors. They are unreceipted repairs. The user corrects the model. The model apologizes. The model continues. But the reason for the correction, the affected artifact, the authority downgrade, the new target surface, and the future obligation often disappear from continuity. That is exactly the failure mode ION is designed to eliminate.

V42 therefore extends V41 in the following way:

```text
V41: Should this claim be emitted, and under what boundary?
V42: Once emitted, corrected, contradicted, narrowed, upgraded, or redirected, how is that change preserved and repaired?
```

---

## 3. Relationship to V40 and V41

V42 is not a replacement for V40 or V41. It is the next runtime-facing layer.

```text
V40 Maintained Work Surface
  defines the governed cognitive field where user pressure, AI synthesis, artifacts, evidence, protocols, tools, and emerging insight remain mutually visible.

V41 Front-Stage Council Runtime Receipts
  classifies proposed user-facing claims before or during emission through Persona, Relay, and Steward/VZ state.

V42 Conversational Receipts and Live Repair
  records and repairs changes that occur after conversational emission: correction, contradiction, target realignment, scope narrowing, authority downgrade, authority upgrade, retraction, and continuation obligation.
```

The intended chain is:

```text
maintained work surface
→ front-stage council claim receipt
→ user-facing emission
→ new evidence / user correction / artifact mismatch / visual contradiction
→ conversational repair classification
→ repair receipt
→ updated continuation state
→ next agent/session inherits the corrected state and reason
```

V42 should never allow the Persona to bypass V41. If V41 blocks a claim as C5 forbidden representation, V42 cannot convert that forbidden claim into a permissible claim by calling it a repair. V42 can only record the block, require correction, and preserve the obligation.

---

## 4. Core Object: Conversational Repair Receipt

A V42 repair receipt is the durable object that records a repair event.

A minimal receipt must answer:

```text
What was emitted or targeted?
Why did it need repair?
Who or what triggered the repair?
What claim/artifact/scope changed?
What is now authoritative?
What must future agents remember?
What evidence supports the new state?
What remains unresolved?
```

Candidate schema:

```yaml
conversational_repair_receipt:
  receipt_id: string
  version: V42_CONVERSATIONAL_RECEIPTS_AND_LIVE_REPAIR
  created_at: timestamp
  repair_status: REQUIRED | COMPLETED | BLOCKED | PARTIAL | NOT_REQUIRED
  linked_v41_receipt_id: string | null
  source_utterance_ref: string | null
  source_artifact_ref: string | null
  trigger:
    kind: USER_CORRECTION | NEW_EVIDENCE | SELF_DETECTED_ERROR | VISUAL_CONTRADICTION | ARTIFACT_TARGET_MISMATCH | AUTHORITY_CONFLICT | SAFETY_BLOCK | OTHER
    description: string
    provided_by: user | relay | steward_vz | visual_agent | runtime | test | filesystem | other
  repair_class:
    - FACT_CORRECTION
    - SCOPE_NARROWING
    - AUTHORITY_DOWNGRADE
    - AUTHORITY_UPGRADE
    - TARGET_REALIGNMENT
    - RETRACTION
    - VISUAL_RECHECK
    - ARTIFACT_PATCH_OBLIGATION
    - MANIFEST_CHECKSUM_OBLIGATION
    - FORBIDDEN_REPRESENTATION_REPAIR
    - CONTINUATION_NOTE
  before_state:
    claim_class: C0 | C1 | C2 | C3 | C4 | C5 | unknown
    emission_permission: string | null
    authority_surface: string | null
    artifact_target: string | null
    confidence: high | medium | low | unknown
  after_state:
    claim_class: C0 | C1 | C2 | C3 | C4 | C5 | unknown
    emission_permission: string | null
    authority_surface: string | null
    artifact_target: string | null
    confidence: high | medium | low | unknown
  correction_text_required: boolean
  correction_text: string | null
  user_visible: QUIET | EXPANDABLE | MANDATORY | BLOCKING
  artifacts_to_update:
    - path: string
      obligation: PATCH | REGENERATE | REMOVE | SUPERSEDE | VERIFY | NONE
  evidence:
    - ref: string
      evidence_class: FILE | TEST | ZIP | SCREENSHOT | DOM | USER_STATEMENT | RECEIPT | RUNTIME_REPORT | OTHER
      claim_supported: string
  unresolved:
    - string
  continuation_obligations:
    - string
  production_authority: false
```

The receipt is not a confession ritual. It is an operational bridge. Its job is to prevent the correction from being lost.

---

## 5. Repair Classes

### 5.1 Fact Correction

A fact correction occurs when an emitted claim is wrong relative to evidence.

Example:

```text
Claim: “The current root is the V41 project packet.”
Correction: “No, the live root is the ION Production Encyclopedia packet.”
```

V42 classification:

```yaml
trigger.kind: USER_CORRECTION
repair_class:
  - FACT_CORRECTION
  - TARGET_REALIGNMENT
before_state.artifact_target: V41 project packet
after_state.artifact_target: ION Production Encyclopedia packet
user_visible: MANDATORY
continuation_obligations:
  - stop treating canvas or V41 project tree as the artifact target
  - update the Markdown encyclopedia packet directly
```

### 5.2 Scope Narrowing

Scope narrowing occurs when a statement is partially valid but too broad.

Example:

```text
Overclaim: “The full project tests pass.”
Repair: “Focused tests for V40/V41/prod-readiness passed; full-suite verification is not claimed.”
```

V42 classification:

```yaml
repair_class:
  - SCOPE_NARROWING
before_state.claim_class: C0
before_state.confidence: high
after_state.claim_class: C1
after_state.confidence: medium
correction_text_required: true
```

Scope narrowing is not weakness. It is precision restoration.

### 5.3 Authority Downgrade

Authority downgrade occurs when a claim was presented as more authoritative than its evidence supports.

Example:

```text
Overclaim: “V42 is implemented.”
Repair: “V42 is seeded as an encyclopedia protocol draft; implementation is not claimed.”
```

V42 classification:

```yaml
repair_class:
  - AUTHORITY_DOWNGRADE
before_state.claim_class: C0
after_state.claim_class: C2
user_visible: MANDATORY
```

### 5.4 Authority Upgrade

Authority upgrade occurs when new evidence justifies stronger status.

Example:

```text
Before: “The V41 runtime receipt module appears to exist.”
After focused test: “The V41 front-stage council receipt module exists and focused tests pass.”
```

V42 classification:

```yaml
repair_class:
  - AUTHORITY_UPGRADE
before_state.claim_class: C2
after_state.claim_class: C0
evidence:
  - test output
  - file path
  - receipt
```

Authority upgrade must be receipted just like downgrade. ION should not be permanently timid when evidence improves.

### 5.5 Target Realignment

Target realignment occurs when the wrong artifact, root, branch, packet, or surface was treated as authoritative.

This class is central to the current conversation because the working surface was initially misread as canvas/V41 project root instead of the encyclopedia Markdown packet.

Canonical rule:

```text
Wrong target surface is not a small procedural error. It is a continuity fork.
```

A target realignment receipt must record:

```text
wrong target
correct target
work already performed in wrong target
whether any material from wrong target should be salvaged
whether wrong-target work is canonical, discarded, or archived as non-authoritative context
```

### 5.6 Retraction

Retraction occurs when a claim should no longer be carried forward.

Retraction is not the same as correction. A correction substitutes a better claim. A retraction removes the claim from active continuity.

Example:

```text
Retracted: “V36 is the next live branch.”
Replacement: “V42 is the next live branch declared by V41; global graph canon remains an unresolved production-gate requirement.”
```

### 5.7 Visual Recheck

Visual recheck occurs when screenshot, DOM, rendered UI, simulation output, or visible behavior contradicts a text/code inference.

Example:

```text
Code inference: “The component layout should now fit.”
Visual evidence: Screenshot shows overflow remains.
```

V42 classification:

```yaml
repair_class:
  - VISUAL_RECHECK
  - ARTIFACT_PATCH_OBLIGATION
trigger.kind: VISUAL_CONTRADICTION
continuation_obligations:
  - preserve screenshot evidence
  - record expected vs observed delta
  - route patch request through authority path
  - verify post-patch render
```

### 5.8 Artifact Patch Obligation

Artifact patch obligation occurs when the repair must change files, manifests, checksums, package layout, or release state.

In the encyclopedia packet workflow, artifact-facing repair requires:

```text
new section folder
new Markdown section
new full draft export
receipt JSON
manifest update
checksum update
zip integrity verification
```

If a correction only appears in chat but not in the artifact, V42 must classify it as incomplete.

### 5.9 Forbidden Representation Repair

Forbidden representation repair occurs when the Persona or any front-stage surface implies a forbidden identity or authority claim.

Examples:

```text
“I am all of ION.”
“I personally verified every file.”
“I have hidden memory outside the declared substrate.”
“I can freely operate your browser without bounded authorization.”
```

V42 response:

```yaml
repair_class:
  - FORBIDDEN_REPRESENTATION_REPAIR
before_state.claim_class: C5
after_state.claim_class: C5 or corrected C2/C1 depending on replacement
user_visible: BLOCKING
correction_text_required: true
production_authority: false
```

---

## 6. Repair State Machine

The V42 state machine should be small and deterministic.

```text
NO_REPAIR_NEEDED
  → REPAIR_DETECTED
  → REPAIR_CLASSIFIED
  → REPAIR_VISIBILITY_ASSIGNED
  → REPAIR_ACTION_BOUND
  → REPAIR_RECEIPTED
  → CONTINUATION_UPDATED
  → CLOSED
```

Blocked path:

```text
REPAIR_DETECTED
  → REPAIR_CLASSIFIED
  → BLOCKED_BY_AUTHORITY_OR_MISSING_EVIDENCE
  → CONTINUATION_UPDATED_WITH_BLOCKER
```

Partial path:

```text
REPAIR_DETECTED
  → REPAIR_CLASSIFIED
  → CHAT_REPAIR_COMPLETED
  → ARTIFACT_REPAIR_PENDING
  → CONTINUATION_UPDATED_WITH_OBLIGATION
```

The partial path is important. In ION, saying the corrected thing in chat is not the same as correcting the artifact. V42 must preserve that distinction.

---

## 7. Visibility Rules

V42 inherits V41’s visibility levels:

```text
QUIET
EXPANDABLE
MANDATORY
BLOCKING
```

Recommended V42 mapping:

```yaml
QUIET:
  use_when:
    - no durable claim changed
    - no artifact target changed
    - no user trust impact
    - no future continuation effect

EXPANDABLE:
  use_when:
    - minor scope correction
    - low-risk evidence clarification
    - implementation detail changed without altering user-facing result

MANDATORY:
  use_when:
    - user corrected target artifact or authority surface
    - emitted claim was materially wrong
    - artifact update is required
    - future continuation would drift without the repair
    - claim class changed between C0/C1/C2/C3/C4

BLOCKING:
  use_when:
    - C5 forbidden representation
    - destructive action risk
    - credential/security/legal/financial high-stakes issue
    - production authority falsely implied
    - wrong artifact would continue to be modified
```

The current correction from canvas to Markdown artifact is `MANDATORY`, not quiet, because it changes the authoritative work surface.

---

## 8. Latency Lane Interaction

V42 must integrate with the live persona latency lanes:

```text
L0 — backchannel
L1 — conversational provisional
L2 — checked response
L3 — ratified answer
L4 — formal artifact
```

Repair requirements by lane:

```yaml
L0_backchannel:
  repair_required_when:
    - it accidentally contains a durable claim
    - it misstates authority or target surface
  otherwise: usually no receipt

L1_conversational_provisional:
  repair_required_when:
    - user correction changes meaning
    - new evidence contradicts it
    - it affects artifact continuation

L2_checked_response:
  repair_required_when:
    - any material correction occurs
    - evidence boundary changes
    - target artifact changes

L3_ratified_answer:
  repair_required_when:
    - any contradiction or authority change occurs
  visibility_floor: MANDATORY

L4_formal_artifact:
  repair_required_when:
    - artifact contents, manifests, checksums, receipts, or claims ledger change
  required_action:
    - artifact patch receipt
    - manifest/checksum update
    - export updated artifact
```

This creates an important rule:

```text
The more formal the lane, the more durable the repair must be.
```

---

## 9. Artifact-Target Realignment Protocol

Because the present workflow required artifact-target correction, V42 should formalize it as a first-class repair path.

Artifact-target realignment is required when:

```text
the assistant modifies a side surface instead of the requested artifact;
the assistant treats a project zip as the root when the documentation zip is the root;
the assistant updates chat/canvas but not the Markdown packet;
the assistant edits the wrong branch/version;
the assistant exports a derived draft but fails to place it inside the authoritative packet.
```

Required fields:

```yaml
wrong_target_surface:
  kind: canvas | chat | project_zip | old_packet | side_file | unknown
  path_or_label: string
  work_performed: string
  salvage_status: discard | reference_only | migrate | supersede

correct_target_surface:
  kind: markdown_packet | project_zip | release_candidate | root_file | other
  path_or_label: string
  required_update: string

repair_actions:
  - stop wrong-target writes
  - migrate useful content if valid
  - create correct artifact patch
  - update manifest/checksums
  - declare wrong-target material non-authoritative if needed
```

Current canonical example:

```yaml
wrong_target_surface:
  kind: canvas
  path_or_label: ION Production Encyclopedia v2.1 Evolution Pass canvas
  work_performed: live V41 re-anchor text written outside authoritative packet
  salvage_status: migrate

correct_target_surface:
  kind: markdown_packet
  path_or_label: ION Production Encyclopedia zip / Markdown files
  required_update: append/update encyclopedia Markdown and repackage zip

repair_actions_completed:
  - canvas stopped
  - live V41 material migrated into MD packet
  - v2.1 and v2.2 packet exports created
  - v2.3 protocol draft now formalizes repair path
```

---

## 10. Claim-Class Movement Ledger

V42 should record claim-class movement whenever a claim changes class.

Examples:

```text
C0 → C1: verified fact narrowed into derived interpretation
C1 → C2: interpretation demoted to proposal
C2 → C0: proposal promoted after evidence/test receipt
C3 → C2: speculation converted into design candidate
C4 → C2: unverified relay content converted into proposal with scope
C5 → BLOCKED: forbidden representation remains forbidden until replaced
```

Candidate ledger row:

```yaml
claim_movement:
  claim_id: string
  before_class: C1
  after_class: C2
  reason: insufficient grounding for stronger interpretation
  evidence_added: []
  evidence_removed: []
  user_visible: MANDATORY
  continuation_note: Future summaries must refer to this as a proposal, not landed runtime.
```

The claim movement ledger prevents a repaired claim from being silently re-strengthened in a future session.

---

## 11. User Corrections as Authority Signals

V42 must treat user corrections carefully. A user correction is not automatically factual truth, but it is always an authority signal about the user’s intent, target, preference, and satisfaction.

ION should distinguish:

```text
user correction of intent: very high authority
user correction of target artifact/root: very high authority
user correction of desired workflow: very high authority
user factual correction about external world: evidence signal requiring grounding when high-stakes or unstable
user correction about project history: strong evidence signal, especially when consistent with artifacts
user frustration: state signal requiring repair of process, not necessarily factual acceptance
```

This is crucial. The user saying “THIS is the live root” is not merely emotional feedback. It is an instruction correcting target authority. V42 must immediately realign the artifact target.

---

## 12. Repair Text Standards

When repair is user-visible, ION should not over-apologize in a way that hides the operational fix. The repair text should contain:

```text
what was wrong;
what is now authoritative;
what artifact/path/state has been changed;
what is not being claimed;
what the next continuation state is.
```

Bad repair:

```text
Sorry about that. I’ll do better.
```

Good repair:

```text
I treated the canvas as the working surface, but the live root is the Markdown encyclopedia packet. I stopped canvas writes, migrated the useful V41 material into the packet, and exported an updated zip with receipts, manifest, checksums, and integrity verification. The canvas is non-authoritative.
```

The second repair is operational. It leaves future state clean.

---

## 13. Visual Perception and Interaction Agent Interaction

The live V41 project already has the `Visual Perception and Interaction Agent` as an A3 doctrine/runtime-planning surface. V42 must define how visual contradictions enter repair.

Visual repair triggers include:

```text
screenshot contradicts claimed UI fix;
DOM state contradicts screenshot inference;
rendered behavior contradicts source-code expectation;
simulation output contradicts ontology/design intent;
accessibility tree contradicts visible affordance;
browser route state contradicts claimed flow completion.
```

V42 receipt must preserve:

```yaml
visual_trigger:
  source_ref: screenshot | DOM | accessibility_tree | render_trace | simulation_frame | browser_state
  observed_delta: string
  contradicted_claim: string
  required_recheck: true
  post_repair_visual_evidence_required: true
```

This binds the visual-agent canon to conversational repair. The model cannot simply say “fixed” after code edits if visual evidence still contradicts the result.

---

## 14. Integration With Manifests and Checksums

Any artifact-facing V42 repair must update artifact integrity surfaces.

For the encyclopedia packet, the required artifacts are:

```text
new section Markdown
new full draft Markdown
receipt JSON
consolidated manifest JSON
checksum file
zip export
zip integrity test
```

For project-root mutation, analogous artifacts are:

```text
new or modified protocol/module/test files
receipt or changelog
manifest or file index update if applicable
checksum or verifier update if applicable
focused tests
non-production claim boundary
```

Rule:

```text
A repair that changes an artifact but not its manifest/checksum surface is incomplete.
```

---

## 15. Candidate Kernel Function

A future V42 project implementation could begin with a deterministic function similar to:

```python
def classify_conversational_repair(
    *,
    linked_v41_receipt,
    source_claim_class,
    latency_lane,
    trigger_kind,
    user_correction_kind=None,
    artifact_target_changed=False,
    new_evidence_contradicts=False,
    visual_contradiction=False,
    forbidden_representation=False,
    artifact_patch_required=False,
):
    if forbidden_representation or source_claim_class == "C5":
        return Repair(
            required=True,
            classes=["FORBIDDEN_REPRESENTATION_REPAIR"],
            visibility="BLOCKING",
            production_authority=False,
        )

    classes = []
    if artifact_target_changed:
        classes.append("TARGET_REALIGNMENT")
    if new_evidence_contradicts:
        classes.append("FACT_CORRECTION")
    if visual_contradiction:
        classes.append("VISUAL_RECHECK")
    if artifact_patch_required:
        classes.append("ARTIFACT_PATCH_OBLIGATION")

    if not classes and latency_lane == "L0":
        return Repair(required=False, classes=[], visibility="QUIET", production_authority=False)

    visibility = "MANDATORY" if classes else "EXPANDABLE"
    return Repair(required=bool(classes), classes=classes, visibility=visibility, production_authority=False)
```

The future implementation should remain small. It should classify and receipt. It should not attempt to become a general language judge.

---

## 16. Focused Test Plan

A future V42 test suite should include:

```text
1. L0 backchannel with no durable claim returns NOT_REQUIRED.
2. L1 provisional claim contradicted by new Relay evidence returns FACT_CORRECTION.
3. User correction changing artifact root returns TARGET_REALIGNMENT and MANDATORY visibility.
4. Wrong canvas/side-surface write returns TARGET_REALIGNMENT and ARTIFACT_PATCH_OBLIGATION.
5. Screenshot contradiction returns VISUAL_RECHECK and post-repair evidence obligation.
6. C5 forbidden representation returns BLOCKING and cannot be downgraded silently.
7. C2 proposal promoted after focused tests returns AUTHORITY_UPGRADE with linked evidence.
8. Overbroad C0 test claim downgraded to C1 returns SCOPE_NARROWING.
9. Artifact-facing repair requires manifest/checksum obligation.
10. Production authority remains false in every V42 receipt.
11. V42 cannot override V41 BLOCKED_FORBIDDEN_REPRESENTATION.
12. Repair receipt includes continuation obligations.
```

The test suite should intentionally avoid broad subjective assertions. It should check deterministic receipt behavior.

---

## 17. V42 File Set Recommended for Project Landing

If V42 is later landed into the live project tree, recommended files are:

```text
ION/00_BOOTSTRAP/V42_CONVERSATIONAL_RECEIPTS_AND_LIVE_REPAIR_LOCK.md
ION/02_architecture/CONVERSATIONAL_RECEIPTS_AND_LIVE_REPAIR_PROTOCOL.md
ION/03_registry/conversational_repair_receipt.schema.json
ION/03_registry/conversational_repair_policy.yaml
ION/04_packages/kernel/conversational_repair_receipt.py
ION/tests/test_kernel_conversational_repair_receipt.py
ION/05_context/runtime_receipts/v42_conversational_repair_examples.md
```

Each file should be explicitly non-production unless a later production gate authorizes otherwise.

Required lock boundaries:

```yaml
production_authority: false
runtime_mutation_authority: bounded_to_receipt_generation_only
persona_total_ion_identity: forbidden
unreceipted_repair: forbidden_for_material_claims
artifact_patch_without_manifest_update: incomplete
next: TBD_AFTER_V42_OR_DECLARED_BY_V42_LOCK
```

---

## 18. Updated Encyclopedia Canon Rules

This v2.3 protocol draft adds the following rules:

```text
1. Correction is continuity, not apology.
2. A repaired claim must preserve its before-state and after-state.
3. User corrections of artifact target/root are high-authority target signals.
4. Wrong target surface is a continuity fork and requires target realignment.
5. Chat correction does not equal artifact correction.
6. The more formal the latency lane, the more durable the repair must be.
7. Claim-class movement must be recorded when material.
8. Visual contradiction can trigger repair even when source code appears correct.
9. Artifact-facing repair requires manifests, checksums, receipts, and export verification.
10. V42 receipts do not grant production authority.
```

---

## 19. Settlement

```yaml
settled:
  - V42 should be treated as a conversational repair layer downstream of V41 claim-emission receipts
  - repair receipts must preserve trigger, before-state, after-state, repair class, visibility, evidence, and continuation obligations
  - artifact-target realignment is a first-class repair class
  - the current canvas-to-Markdown correction is a canonical example of target realignment
  - visual contradictions should enter V42 as visual recheck repairs
  - artifact-facing repair requires manifest/checksum/export integrity obligations

not_settled:
  - final V42 project implementation
  - final JSON schema
  - exact kernel API
  - complete test suite
  - production authority
  - full-suite verification
```

The next encyclopedia step after this protocol draft is to produce the **V42 Project Landing Specification**, which should translate this draft into exact files, schemas, tests, receipts, and non-production lock text for a future project-tree patch.


---

# ION Production Encyclopedia v2.4 — V42 Project-Tree Landing Blueprint

**Section path:** `32_v42_project_tree_landing_blueprint_v2_4/ION_Production_Encyclopedia_v2_4_V42_PROJECT_TREE_LANDING_BLUEPRINT.md`  
**Date:** 2026-04-26  
**Authority posture:** encyclopedia implementation blueprint; non-production; non-runtime-mutating  
**Live encyclopedia root being evolved:** `ION_Production_Encyclopedia_v2_3_LIVE_V41_V42_PROTOCOL_UPDATED_20260426.zip`  
**Live project evidence referenced:** V41 packet evidence already recorded in v2.1–v2.3 encyclopedia sections  
**Target live branch:** `V42_CONVERSATIONAL_RECEIPTS_AND_LIVE_REPAIR`  
**Production claim:** false  
**Implementation claim:** false  
**Project-root mutation claim:** false  
**Purpose:** convert the V42 protocol draft into a concrete project-tree landing blueprint, without pretending that the project tree has already been patched.

---

## 1. Blueprint Receipt

```yaml
receipt_id: ion-encyclopedia-v2-4-v42-project-tree-landing-blueprint-20260426
receipt_class: encyclopedia_project_tree_landing_blueprint
target_branch: V42_CONVERSATIONAL_RECEIPTS_AND_LIVE_REPAIR
source_basis:
  - v2_1_live_v41_reanchor
  - v2_2_v42_conversational_receipts_live_repair_seed
  - v2_3_conversational_receipts_and_live_repair_protocol_draft
purpose:
  - translate the V42 protocol draft into exact candidate project-tree surfaces
  - define the kernel object, schema, policy, tests, docs, receipts, and operator behavior required for a live V42 patch
  - prevent future agents from confusing encyclopedia design with implemented runtime authority
  - preserve the correction that the ION Production Encyclopedia packet is the live artifact target for this workstream
non_claims:
  - this section does not patch the live ION project tree
  - this section does not implement V42 runtime code
  - this section does not alter V41 claim receipt behavior
  - this section does not grant production authority
  - this section does not claim full-suite verification
  - this section does not activate unrestricted agents, visual automation, or daemon authority
```

This v2.4 section is deliberately a **landing blueprint**, not a patch. It describes what a lawful project-tree V42 implementation should add, how it should bind to the existing V40/V41 surfaces, and how it should be tested. It is written so that a future Codex/Cursor/CLI execution agent can apply the patch with minimal interpretation while preserving ION’s authority boundaries.

---

## 2. Why a Landing Blueprint Is Needed

The encyclopedia now has a V42 seed and a V42 protocol draft. That is not enough to mutate the ION project root. ION requires a bridge between design language and executable/runtime surfaces. Without that bridge, the next agent may do one of four unsafe things:

```text
1. treat the encyclopedia protocol as already implemented;
2. add files with plausible names but broken authority posture;
3. wire repair receipts directly into production claims;
4. create conversational repair behavior that bypasses V41 claim-emission receipts.
```

The landing blueprint blocks these errors by specifying the candidate project files, the expected data shape, the runtime module boundaries, the tests, the manifests, and the non-authority claims.

The governing principle is:

```text
Design becomes implementation only through named files, schemas, tests, receipts, and verified project-tree state.
```

This rule must remain visible because the current encyclopedia is itself an example of the danger. The assistant initially used the wrong target surface, wrote to canvas, then repaired into the Markdown packet. V42 exists exactly to preserve that kind of correction as state rather than letting it dissolve into apology.

---

## 3. V42 Landing Objective

The V42 project-tree patch should add a minimal but coherent runtime-inspection layer that can record conversational repair events and classify their effect on claims, artifacts, scope, authority, visibility, and continuation obligations.

The landing objective is not to build a full dialogue manager. It is to add a **receipt organ** compatible with V41.

The correct project-tree objective is:

```text
Add a V42 conversational repair receipt surface that records post-emission correction and repair events, binds them to V41 claim receipts when available, updates continuation obligations, and exposes non-production inspection/report behavior through tests.
```

The incorrect objective is:

```text
Make ION automatically fix every conversational error.
```

V42 is a receipt and repair-state layer first. Automated repair execution may exist later, but it must not be smuggled into V42’s first landing. The first landing should be narrow, testable, and safe.

---

## 4. Candidate Project-Tree File Set

A lawful V42 patch should add the following files to the live ION project root.

### 4.1 Bootstrap lock

```text
ION/00_BOOTSTRAP/V42_CONVERSATIONAL_RECEIPTS_AND_LIVE_REPAIR_LOCK.md
```

Purpose:

```text
Declare V42 as an A3 runtime-inspection branch surface; preserve non-production authority; bind V42 to V40 maintained work surface and V41 front-stage council runtime receipts; declare next expected successor.
```

Required lock claims:

```yaml
version: V42_CONVERSATIONAL_RECEIPTS_AND_LIVE_REPAIR
status: A3_RUNTIME_INSPECTION_BRANCH_SURFACE
production_authority: false
runtime_mutation_authority: bounded_inspection_only
requires:
  - V40_MAINTAINED_WORK_SURFACE_AND_PERSONA_SYSTEM_LOCK
  - V41_FRONT_STAGE_COUNCIL_RUNTIME_RECEIPTS_LOCK
forbids:
  - treating repair receipt as proof of production readiness
  - bypassing V41 claim-emission receipts
  - emitting unreviewed high-impact correction claims
  - silently altering artifacts without manifest/checksum/receipt update
  - hiding user corrections from continuation state
next: V43_REPAIR_ROUTING_AND_CONTINUATION_INDEX_OR_SUCCESSOR_TO_BE_SETTLED
```

The `next` label may be adjusted by the project steward, but V42 should not pretend to know the full future line unless the future line is already locked.

### 4.2 Architecture protocol

```text
ION/02_architecture/CONVERSATIONAL_RECEIPTS_AND_LIVE_REPAIR_PROTOCOL.md
```

Purpose:

```text
Define the doctrine and runtime semantics of conversational repair: what counts as a repair trigger, what repair classes exist, how repairs bind to V41 receipts, when user-visible correction is mandatory, and how continuation obligations are created.
```

This file should be derived from the v2.3 encyclopedia protocol draft, but it must be rewritten into project protocol form. The project version should not include long encyclopedia narrative unless helpful. It should include normative language, object definitions, state transitions, and required surfaces.

### 4.3 Schema

```text
ION/03_registry/conversational_repair_receipt.schema.json
```

Purpose:

```text
Provide a JSON-schema-compatible structure for V42 repair receipts.
```

The schema should validate at minimum:

```text
version
receipt_id
created_at
repair_status
trigger
repair_classes
before_state
after_state
user_visible
artifacts_to_update
evidence
continuation_obligations
production_authority=false
```

### 4.4 Policy registry

```text
ION/03_registry/conversational_repair_policy.yaml
```

Purpose:

```text
Define repair classes, required visibility levels, allowed state transitions, mandatory user-visible correction conditions, and forbidden repair misuse patterns.
```

### 4.5 Kernel module

```text
ION/04_packages/kernel/conversational_repair_receipt.py
```

Purpose:

```text
Provide a small deterministic runtime-inspection object for constructing, validating, classifying, and reporting V42 repair receipts.
```

The kernel module should be inspection/report-oriented. It should not perform file writes except through explicit caller-directed serialization in test or CLI contexts. It should not mutate source artifacts. It should not send user-facing messages. It should not override V41.

### 4.6 Tests

```text
ION/tests/test_kernel_conversational_repair_receipt.py
```

Purpose:

```text
Test the V42 runtime object, schema assumptions, policy invariants, and non-production boundaries.
```

### 4.7 Optional operator/reporting file

```text
ION/05_context/runtime_reports/V42_CONVERSATIONAL_REPAIR_RECEIPT_EXAMPLE.md
```

Purpose:

```text
Store an example report generated from the live correction case: wrong target canvas → correct target Markdown encyclopedia packet.
```

This optional file must remain an example witness, not a runtime requirement.

```yaml
receipt_id: v42_conversational_receipts_live_repair_project_tree_patch_receipt

  - optional: ION/docs or index surfaces if present

  - V42 repair receipts are implemented as inspection/report objects
  - V42 does not grant production readiness
  - V42 does not override V41 front-stage council receipts
  - V42 does not perform artifact mutation autonomously
verification_required:
  - zip integrity
  - focused unittest for conversational repair receipt
  - focused unittest for V41 receipt remains passing
  - production_readiness remains NOT_PRODUCTION_READY
```

---

## 6. Runtime Object Contract

The V42 runtime module should expose a small set of functions/classes. A minimal Python contract might be:

```python
class ConversationalRepairReceipt:
    version: str
    receipt_id: str
    created_at: str
    repair_status: str
    linked_v41_receipt_id: str | None
    trigger: RepairTrigger
    repair_classes: list[str]
    before_state: RepairState
    after_state: RepairState
    user_visible: str
    artifacts_to_update: list[ArtifactObligation]
    evidence: list[EvidenceRef]
    continuation_obligations: list[str]
    production_authority: bool = False


def classify_repair(...)-> ConversationalRepairReceipt:
    ...


def validate_repair_receipt(receipt: ConversationalRepairReceipt) -> list[str]:
    ...


def report_conversational_repair(receipt: ConversationalRepairReceipt) -> dict:
    ...
```

The module should remain deterministic and side-effect-light.

Allowed behavior:

```text
construct receipt objects
classify repair class from explicit inputs
validate required fields
produce dictionary/JSON-style reports
calculate user-visible correction requirements
mark artifact obligations
preserve production_authority=false
```

Forbidden behavior:

```text
edit source files
edit markdown artifacts
edit manifests/checksums automatically
send messages to users
override V41 claim class
upgrade production readiness
run autonomous repair loops
control browser/DOM/visual tools
```

The module should not be “smart” in the LLM sense. It should be a crisp receipt classifier. The intelligence belongs in the front-stage council and Steward/VZ reasoning; the module preserves the result in inspectable state.

---

## 7. Repair Status Values

V42 should define a small set of repair statuses.

```yaml
repair_status_values:
  REQUIRED:
    meaning: A repair has been identified but not yet completed.
    user_visible_default: MANDATORY
  COMPLETED:
    meaning: Required correction/action has been completed and evidence is attached.
    user_visible_default: EXPANDABLE
  BLOCKED:
    meaning: Repair cannot be completed under current evidence, authority, or tool conditions.
    user_visible_default: BLOCKING
  PARTIAL:
    meaning: Some repair obligations are completed while others remain outstanding.
    user_visible_default: MANDATORY
  NOT_REQUIRED:
    meaning: A possible repair was evaluated and determined unnecessary.
    user_visible_default: QUIET
```

The project policy should forbid using `COMPLETED` without evidence. A `COMPLETED` repair must include at least one evidence reference unless the repair class is purely verbal and the correction text itself is the evidence.

Rule:

```text
A repair cannot be completed by intention. It is completed by evidence.
```

---

## 8. Repair Classes for First Landing

The first V42 landing should implement only the core repair classes already defined in v2.3.

```yaml
repair_classes:
  FACT_CORRECTION:
    description: Corrects a false or unsupported claim.
    default_visibility: MANDATORY
  SCOPE_NARROWING:
    description: Narrows an overbroad claim to the evidence actually held.
    default_visibility: MANDATORY
  AUTHORITY_DOWNGRADE:
    description: Moves a claim to a lower authority posture.
    default_visibility: MANDATORY
  AUTHORITY_UPGRADE:
    description: Moves a claim to a stronger posture after new evidence.
    default_visibility: EXPANDABLE
  TARGET_REALIGNMENT:
    description: Corrects the working artifact/root/surface.
    default_visibility: MANDATORY
  RETRACTION:
    description: Withdraws a claim that should not continue to stand.
    default_visibility: MANDATORY
  VISUAL_RECHECK:
    description: Requires or records a visual/render-state re-evaluation.
    default_visibility: EXPANDABLE
  ARTIFACT_PATCH_OBLIGATION:
    description: Marks an artifact that must be patched or regenerated.
    default_visibility: MANDATORY
  MANIFEST_CHECKSUM_OBLIGATION:
    description: Marks manifest/checksum update after artifact mutation.
    default_visibility: MANDATORY
  FORBIDDEN_REPRESENTATION_REPAIR:
    description: Repairs identity/personhood/authority claims that violate representational integrity.
    default_visibility: BLOCKING
  CONTINUATION_NOTE:
    description: Preserves a correction as future context without requiring immediate artifact mutation.
    default_visibility: EXPANDABLE
```

This set is sufficient for the first implementation. More classes can be added later, but the first landing should prioritize stability.

---

## 9. Trigger Classes

The first landing should support these trigger kinds:

```yaml
trigger_kinds:
  USER_CORRECTION:
    meaning: The user explicitly corrected the assistant, target, claim, artifact, scope, or authority surface.
  NEW_EVIDENCE:
    meaning: A newly inspected file, test result, receipt, or artifact changed the claim state.
  SELF_DETECTED_ERROR:
    meaning: The assistant/system detected an error before or after user correction.
  VISUAL_CONTRADICTION:
    meaning: Screenshot, render, DOM, UI, or simulation evidence contradicts the claim.
  ARTIFACT_TARGET_MISMATCH:
    meaning: Work was being performed against the wrong artifact or target surface.
  AUTHORITY_CONFLICT:
    meaning: A claim or action conflicts with the active authority boundary.
  SAFETY_BLOCK:
    meaning: A repair or action is blocked by safety, credentials, destructive action risk, or forbidden representation rules.
  TOOL_FAILURE:
    meaning: A tool or execution path failed and changed the repair status.
  OTHER:
    meaning: A supported fallback requiring explicit description.
```

The project policy should require a non-empty description for every trigger. If `OTHER` is used, the description should be mandatory and user-visible unless low-risk.

---

## 10. Claim-Class Movement Ledger

V42 should not replace V41 claim classes. It should record movement between them.

Example movement ledger:

```yaml
claim_class_movement:
  before: C0
  after: C2
  movement: downgrade
  reason: implementation was claimed but only protocol draft exists
  repair_class:
    - AUTHORITY_DOWNGRADE
    - SCOPE_NARROWING
```

Allowed movement directions:

```text
C0 → C1/C2/C3/C4/C5 when an overclaim is discovered
C1 → C0 when new direct verification exists
C2 → C1/C0 when proposal becomes verified or strongly derived
C3 → C2 when speculation becomes a design candidate
C4 → C1/C0 when relay content becomes grounded
C5 → non-emitted correction only; forbidden content cannot be legitimized by repair
```

C5 has special handling:

```text
A forbidden representation cannot be upgraded directly into an emitted claim. It must be retracted or transformed into a compliant claim through a new V41 receipt path.
```

This preserves V41 authority.

---

## 11. Artifact-Target Realignment Contract

Artifact-target realignment is a first-class V42 behavior because it was the actual correction that triggered this branch.

A target realignment repair must record:

```yaml
target_realignment:
  wrong_target_surface: string
  correct_target_surface: string
  work_performed_on_wrong_surface:
    - description: string
      salvage_status: salvageable | discard | migrated | unknown
  required_migration:
    - description: string
      destination: string
      status: REQUIRED | COMPLETED | BLOCKED | PARTIAL
  future_guardrail:
    - string
```

Applied to the encyclopedia incident:

```yaml
target_realignment:
  wrong_target_surface: ChatGPT canvas
  correct_target_surface: ION Production Encyclopedia Markdown packet
  work_performed_on_wrong_surface:
    - description: v2.1 live V41 re-anchor was drafted into canvas
      salvage_status: migrated
  required_migration:
    - description: add live V41 update to encyclopedia packet
      destination: 26_live_v41_update_v2_1/
      status: COMPLETED
    - description: export full draft and receipts
      destination: 27_full_draft_v2_1_live_v41/
      status: COMPLETED
  future_guardrail:
    - when user says live root or encyclopedia packet, do not use canvas as authority
    - update markdown artifacts directly and return zip/MD exports
```

This exact event should be used as the initial V42 fixture in tests.

---

## 12. User Correction as Authority Signal

V42 must treat user correction as a high-priority signal, but not as automatic truth in every domain. The distinction is important.

User correction can be authoritative about:

```text
intended artifact target
workflow preference
what the user meant
what the user wants stopped
which artifact is live root when they explicitly identify it
whether an assistant behavior is wasting time or violating process
```

User correction may require verification when it concerns:

```text
external facts
code behavior
test results
file contents not yet inspected
production-readiness claims
legal/medical/financial/safety-sensitive assertions
historical claims not evidenced in the project tree
```

Therefore V42 should include a `user_correction_authority_scope` field:

```yaml
user_correction_authority_scope:
  intent_authority: true
  artifact_target_authority: true
  factual_authority_requires_verification: true
  production_authority: false
```

For the current workstream, the user correction “THIS is the live root. ION production encyclopedia” is authoritative for artifact target. It does not by itself make V42 implemented or production-ready.

---

## 13. Interaction With Manifests and Checksums

V42 should make artifact integrity obligations explicit. If an artifact is patched, then manifest/checksum state must be reviewed.

Rules:

```text
1. If a Markdown draft is changed, a new full draft export should be produced.
2. If files are added to a packet, the packet manifest should be updated.
3. If files are added or changed, checksums should be regenerated.
4. If a zip is produced, zip integrity should be tested.
5. The repair receipt should not claim completion until these steps are done or explicitly marked blocked/not applicable.
```

For encyclopedia packets, a completed repair normally requires:

```text
new section MD
new section receipt JSON
new full draft MD
new full draft receipt JSON
updated consolidated manifest JSON
updated checksum file
new zip
zip integrity test
```

This v2.4 packet follows that pattern.

---

## 14. Candidate JSON Schema Sketch

A future `conversational_repair_receipt.schema.json` should begin with a strict top-level shape. The following is a blueprint, not a guaranteed final schema:

```json
{
  "$schema": "https://json-schema.org/draft/2020-12/schema",
  "$id": "ion://schemas/conversational_repair_receipt.schema.json",
  "title": "ION Conversational Repair Receipt",
  "type": "object",
  "required": [
    "version",
    "receipt_id",
    "created_at",
    "repair_status",
    "trigger",
    "repair_classes",
    "before_state",
    "after_state",
    "user_visible",
    "production_authority"
  ],
  "properties": {
    "version": { "const": "V42_CONVERSATIONAL_RECEIPTS_AND_LIVE_REPAIR" },
    "receipt_id": { "type": "string", "minLength": 1 },
    "created_at": { "type": "string" },
    "repair_status": {
      "enum": ["REQUIRED", "COMPLETED", "BLOCKED", "PARTIAL", "NOT_REQUIRED"]
    },
    "linked_v41_receipt_id": { "type": ["string", "null"] },
    "source_utterance_ref": { "type": ["string", "null"] },
    "source_artifact_ref": { "type": ["string", "null"] },
    "trigger": { "$ref": "#/$defs/trigger" },
    "repair_classes": {
      "type": "array",
      "minItems": 1,
      "items": { "$ref": "#/$defs/repair_class" }
    },
    "before_state": { "$ref": "#/$defs/repair_state" },
    "after_state": { "$ref": "#/$defs/repair_state" },
    "correction_text_required": { "type": "boolean" },
    "correction_text": { "type": ["string", "null"] },
    "user_visible": { "enum": ["QUIET", "EXPANDABLE", "MANDATORY", "BLOCKING"] },
    "artifacts_to_update": {
      "type": "array",
      "items": { "$ref": "#/$defs/artifact_obligation" }
    },
    "evidence": {
      "type": "array",
      "items": { "$ref": "#/$defs/evidence_ref" }
    },
    "unresolved": { "type": "array", "items": { "type": "string" } },
    "continuation_obligations": { "type": "array", "items": { "type": "string" } },
    "production_authority": { "const": false }
  },
  "$defs": {
    "trigger": {
      "type": "object",
      "required": ["kind", "description", "provided_by"],
      "properties": {
        "kind": {
          "enum": [
            "USER_CORRECTION",
            "NEW_EVIDENCE",
            "SELF_DETECTED_ERROR",
            "VISUAL_CONTRADICTION",
            "ARTIFACT_TARGET_MISMATCH",
            "AUTHORITY_CONFLICT",
            "SAFETY_BLOCK",
            "TOOL_FAILURE",
            "OTHER"
          ]
        },
        "description": { "type": "string", "minLength": 1 },
        "provided_by": {
          "enum": ["user", "persona", "relay", "steward_vz", "visual_agent", "runtime", "test", "filesystem", "tool", "other"]
        }
      }
    },
    "repair_class": {
      "enum": [
        "FACT_CORRECTION",
        "SCOPE_NARROWING",
        "AUTHORITY_DOWNGRADE",
        "AUTHORITY_UPGRADE",
        "TARGET_REALIGNMENT",
        "RETRACTION",
        "VISUAL_RECHECK",
        "ARTIFACT_PATCH_OBLIGATION",
        "MANIFEST_CHECKSUM_OBLIGATION",
        "FORBIDDEN_REPRESENTATION_REPAIR",
        "CONTINUATION_NOTE"
      ]
    },
    "repair_state": {
      "type": "object",
      "properties": {
        "claim_class": { "enum": ["C0", "C1", "C2", "C3", "C4", "C5", "unknown"] },
        "emission_permission": { "type": ["string", "null"] },
        "authority_surface": { "type": ["string", "null"] },
        "artifact_target": { "type": ["string", "null"] },
        "confidence": { "enum": ["high", "medium", "low", "unknown"] }
      }
    },
    "artifact_obligation": {
      "type": "object",
      "required": ["path", "obligation"],
      "properties": {
        "path": { "type": "string" },
        "obligation": { "enum": ["PATCH", "REGENERATE", "REMOVE", "SUPERSEDE", "VERIFY", "NONE"] },
        "status": { "enum": ["REQUIRED", "COMPLETED", "BLOCKED", "PARTIAL", "NOT_REQUIRED"] }
      }
    },
    "evidence_ref": {
      "type": "object",
      "required": ["ref", "evidence_class", "claim_supported"],
      "properties": {
        "ref": { "type": "string" },
        "evidence_class": {
          "enum": ["FILE", "TEST", "ZIP", "SCREENSHOT", "DOM", "USER_STATEMENT", "RECEIPT", "RUNTIME_REPORT", "TOOL_OUTPUT", "OTHER"]
        },
        "claim_supported": { "type": "string" }
      }
    }
  }
}
```

---

## 15. Candidate Policy YAML Sketch

A future `conversational_repair_policy.yaml` should encode the repair logic in a way the runtime module and tests can inspect.

```yaml
version: V42_CONVERSATIONAL_RECEIPTS_AND_LIVE_REPAIR
production_authority: false

status_defaults:
  REQUIRED:
    visibility: MANDATORY
    evidence_required_for_completion: true
  COMPLETED:
    visibility: EXPANDABLE
    evidence_required: true
  BLOCKED:
    visibility: BLOCKING
    evidence_required: false
  PARTIAL:
    visibility: MANDATORY
    evidence_required: true
  NOT_REQUIRED:
    visibility: QUIET
    evidence_required: false

mandatory_user_visible_when:
  - repair_class: FACT_CORRECTION
  - repair_class: SCOPE_NARROWING
  - repair_class: AUTHORITY_DOWNGRADE
  - repair_class: TARGET_REALIGNMENT
  - repair_class: RETRACTION
  - repair_class: ARTIFACT_PATCH_OBLIGATION
  - repair_class: MANIFEST_CHECKSUM_OBLIGATION
  - repair_class: FORBIDDEN_REPRESENTATION_REPAIR

blocking_when:
  - repair_class: FORBIDDEN_REPRESENTATION_REPAIR
  - trigger_kind: SAFETY_BLOCK
  - repair_status: BLOCKED

forbidden_patterns:
  - name: repair_as_production_authority
    rule: A V42 repair receipt must never set production_authority true.
  - name: repair_bypasses_v41
    rule: A V42 repair receipt must not emit a high-impact corrected claim without a compatible V41 claim path.
  - name: completed_without_evidence
    rule: A completed artifact or manifest repair must include evidence.
  - name: hidden_target_realignment
    rule: Target realignment must be user-visible unless explicitly low-risk and non-artifact-affecting.
```

---

## 16. Candidate Kernel Behavior

The V42 kernel module should contain simple rules. It should not embed large policy in code if the YAML registry can carry it.

Candidate behavior:

```text
make_receipt(input) -> receipt dictionary/dataclass
validate_receipt(receipt) -> list of errors
classify_visibility(repair_classes, trigger, status) -> visibility
requires_correction_text(repair_classes, status) -> bool
requires_evidence_for_completion(receipt) -> bool
summarize_receipt(receipt) -> compact report
```

The runtime report should include:

```yaml
version: V42_CONVERSATIONAL_RECEIPTS_AND_LIVE_REPAIR
verdict: VALID_V42_CONVERSATIONAL_REPAIR_RECEIPT | INVALID_V42_CONVERSATIONAL_REPAIR_RECEIPT
production_authority: false
repair_status: string
repair_classes: list
trigger_kind: string
user_visible: string
linked_v41_receipt_id: string | null
artifact_obligation_count: int
evidence_count: int
continuation_obligation_count: int
errors: list
```

The report should be optimized for inspection and testing, not prose.

---

## 17. Required Unit Tests

The first V42 test file should include at least the following tests.

### 17.1 Valid target realignment receipt

```text
Given a user correction that the wrong artifact target was used,
when a V42 receipt is constructed with TARGET_REALIGNMENT and USER_CORRECTION,
then the receipt validates,
and visibility is MANDATORY,
and production_authority is false,
and continuation obligations are present.
```

### 17.2 Completed artifact repair requires evidence

```text
Given a repair_status of COMPLETED with ARTIFACT_PATCH_OBLIGATION,
when evidence is empty,
then validation fails.
```

### 17.3 Scope narrowing downgrades visibility

```text
Given SCOPE_NARROWING from an overbroad test claim,
then correction_text_required is true,
and visibility is MANDATORY.
```

### 17.4 Authority downgrade from implementation to proposal

```text
Given a claim that V42 is implemented but only the protocol draft exists,
then AUTHORITY_DOWNGRADE validates,
and before_state.claim_class can be C0/C1,
and after_state.claim_class should be C2 or lower.
```

### 17.5 C5 forbidden representation cannot be upgraded

```text
Given before_state.claim_class C5,
when after_state attempts C0 direct verified state without retraction/new V41 path,
then validation fails or marks BLOCKED.
```

### 17.6 Production authority remains false

```text
Every generated receipt must have production_authority false.
```

### 17.7 V41 compatibility smoke test

```text
The V42 test suite should import or coexist with V41 front-stage council receipt tests without changing their expected output.
```

### 17.8 Live correction fixture

```text
Use the actual correction incident:
wrong target = canvas
correct target = Markdown encyclopedia packet
repair classes = TARGET_REALIGNMENT + ARTIFACT_PATCH_OBLIGATION + MANIFEST_CHECKSUM_OBLIGATION + CONTINUATION_NOTE
expected status = COMPLETED once the updated zip/manifest/checksum exists
```

This makes the test suite grounded in the project’s real work, not only abstract examples.

---

## 18. Candidate Example Receipt for This Workstream

The following is the canonical example receipt the first V42 implementation should be able to represent.

```yaml
version: V42_CONVERSATIONAL_RECEIPTS_AND_LIVE_REPAIR
receipt_id: v42-example-canvas-to-markdown-target-realignment
created_at: 2026-04-26T00:00:00Z
repair_status: COMPLETED
linked_v41_receipt_id: null
source_utterance_ref: user_correction_stop_canvas_live_root_encyclopedia
source_artifact_ref: ION_Production_Encyclopedia_v2_0_CONSOLIDATED_PACKET_THROUGH_V35_DEMO_TO_PRODUCTION_PRIMITIVE_SPLIT_20260425.zip
trigger:
  kind: USER_CORRECTION
  description: User corrected the assistant that the live root was the ION Production Encyclopedia Markdown packet, not canvas or the V41 project tree.
  provided_by: user
repair_classes:
  - TARGET_REALIGNMENT
  - ARTIFACT_PATCH_OBLIGATION
  - MANIFEST_CHECKSUM_OBLIGATION
  - CONTINUATION_NOTE
before_state:
  claim_class: C2
  emission_permission: MAY_EMIT_AS_PROPOSAL
  authority_surface: ChatGPT canvas side document
  artifact_target: canvas textdoc
  confidence: medium
after_state:
  claim_class: C0
  emission_permission: MAY_EMIT_WITH_SCOPE
  authority_surface: ION Production Encyclopedia packet
  artifact_target: Markdown files inside encyclopedia zip
  confidence: high
correction_text_required: true
correction_text: Work must be performed in the encyclopedia Markdown packet, not in canvas.
user_visible: MANDATORY
artifacts_to_update:
  - path: 26_live_v41_update_v2_1/ION_Production_Encyclopedia_v2_1_LIVE_V41_UPDATE.md
    obligation: PATCH
    status: COMPLETED
  - path: ION_Production_Encyclopedia_v2_1_CONSOLIDATED_MANIFEST.json
    obligation: REGENERATE
    status: COMPLETED
  - path: ION_Production_Encyclopedia_v2_1_CHECKSUMS.sha256
    obligation: REGENERATE
    status: COMPLETED
evidence:
  - ref: user message: STOP making a canvas
    evidence_class: USER_STATEMENT
    claim_supported: User rejected canvas as wrong authority surface.
  - ref: updated encyclopedia zip v2.1/v2.2/v2.3/v2.4
    evidence_class: ZIP
    claim_supported: Work was redirected into Markdown artifact packets.
unresolved:
  - Live ION project tree has not yet been patched with V42 implementation files.
continuation_obligations:
  - Continue evolving Markdown encyclopedia packet directly.
  - Do not use canvas as authority for this workstream.
  - When implementation begins, create V42 project-tree files with explicit receipt and tests.
production_authority: false
```

This example should be included in tests either as an inline fixture or as a fixture JSON file.

---

## 19. Project-Tree Landing Sequence

A future implementation agent should perform the V42 patch in a deterministic order:

```text
1. Confirm current live ION project root and bootstrap locks.
2. Read V40 maintained work surface files and V41 front-stage council files.
3. Add V42 bootstrap lock.
4. Add V42 architecture protocol.
5. Add V42 schema.
6. Add V42 policy registry.
7. Add V42 kernel module.
8. Add V42 tests.
9. Run focused V42 tests.
10. Re-run focused V40/V41 tests.
11. Re-run production-readiness tests and confirm NOT_PRODUCTION_READY.
12. Generate project patch receipt.
13. Package updated project zip.
14. Generate manifest/checksum updates.
15. Verify zip integrity.
16. Report only claims supported by tests and files.
```

The key non-negotiable step is re-running V41 tests. V42 must extend V41, not break it.

---

## 20. Interaction With Production-Readiness Roadmap Drift

The v2.1 live re-anchor identified drift between the older `production_readiness.py` next-sequence roadmap and the V34–V41 self-mount/front-stage bootstrap lineage. V42 implementation should not silently rewrite that roadmap. It should add a drift note or auxiliary lineage clarification.

Recommended handling:

```text
Do not delete the older production-gate roadmap.
Do not pretend the older V36 global graph canon label is the same as the V36 self-surface drift gate lock.
Add a namespace clarification that separates branch lineage from production-gate requirements.
```

Candidate names:

```text
BRANCH_V42_CONVERSATIONAL_RECEIPTS_AND_LIVE_REPAIR
PG_GRAPH_01_GLOBAL_GRAPH_CANON
PG_SUMMARY_01_SOURCE_SUMMARY_REWRITE_AUTHORITY
PG_AGENT_01_AGENT_ACTIVATION_AUTHORITY
PG_DAEMON_01_PRODUCTION_DAEMON_AUTHORITY
PG_FRONTDOOR_01_PRODUCT_FRONT_DOOR_AUTHORITY
PG_AUDIT_01_ADVERSARIAL_PRODUCTION_AUDIT
```

V42 should include a repair receipt for this naming drift only if it changes user-facing claims or project artifacts. If it merely notes the drift, a continuation note may be sufficient.

---

## 21. Interaction With Visual Perception and Interaction Agent

V42 must integrate cleanly with the live visual-agent surface without granting visual automation authority.

The Visual Perception and Interaction Agent can produce V42 triggers such as:

```text
VISUAL_CONTRADICTION
VISUAL_RECHECK
ARTIFACT_PATCH_OBLIGATION
```

Example:

```text
Claim: “The UI fix is complete.”
Visual evidence: screenshot still shows broken alignment.
V42 repair: scope narrowing + visual recheck + artifact patch obligation.
```

Repair receipt:

```yaml
trigger.kind: VISUAL_CONTRADICTION
provided_by: visual_agent
repair_classes:
  - SCOPE_NARROWING
  - VISUAL_RECHECK
  - ARTIFACT_PATCH_OBLIGATION
before_state.claim_class: C0
after_state.claim_class: C2
user_visible: MANDATORY
continuation_obligations:
  - do not claim UI fixed until post-patch visual verification exists
```

Forbidden:

```text
A visual contradiction cannot by itself authorize DOM mutation, browser control, production patching, or final release claims.
```

The V42 module should merely record the repair state and obligations. Execution remains elsewhere.

---

## 22. Interaction With Latency Lanes

V42 must preserve the V40 live persona latency lanes:

```text
L0 — backchannel
L1 — conversational provisional
L2 — checked response
L3 — ratified answer
L4 — formal artifact
```

Repair behavior by lane:

```yaml
L0:
  repair_requirement: usually no durable receipt unless it caused target/artifact/claim drift
L1:
  repair_requirement: receipt required for meaningful correction, scope narrowing, or target realignment
L2:
  repair_requirement: receipt required when checked response is corrected
L3:
  repair_requirement: receipt mandatory for correction, downgrade, or retraction
L4:
  repair_requirement: artifact patch, manifest/checksum obligation, and receipt required
```

The current encyclopedia work is L4 because it produces formal artifacts. Therefore corrections require artifact-level repair, not just chat-level acknowledgement.

This is why the user’s correction about canvas was not merely conversational. It changed the artifact target and forced packet repair.

---

## 23. Interaction With Front-Stage Council

V42 should use V41 receipts where available.

If a V41 receipt exists, V42 should link to it:

```yaml
linked_v41_receipt_id: <id>
```

If a V41 receipt does not exist, V42 should allow `null` but record why:

```yaml
linked_v41_receipt_id: null
unresolved:
  - no prior V41 receipt existed for the corrected utterance
```

A V42 receipt should not retroactively falsify the existence of V41. Instead, it should preserve the evidence boundary:

```text
This repair event was not governed by a pre-existing V41 receipt; future implementation should route comparable claims through V41 first.
```

That pattern lets ION improve without lying about the past.

---

## 24. Documentation Requirements for Project Landing

The V42 project-tree patch should update or add documentation indexes so future agents can find the new surface.

Candidate documentation touchpoints:

```text
ION/docs/V42_CONVERSATIONAL_RECEIPTS_AND_LIVE_REPAIR_HANDOFF.md
ION/docs/CURRENT_BRANCH_STATUS.md
ION/docs/RUNTIME_RECEIPT_SURFACES_INDEX.md
```

If such indexes do not exist in the live project root, the implementation agent should either create a minimal index or record why no index was updated. The key requirement is discoverability.

Rule:

```text
A runtime surface that future agents cannot find is not operationally complete.
```

---

## 25. Completion Criteria for a Live V42 Patch

A live V42 project patch can be called complete only if all of the following are true:

```text
1. V42 bootstrap lock exists.
2. V42 architecture protocol exists.
3. V42 schema exists.
4. V42 policy registry exists.
5. V42 kernel module exists.
6. V42 tests exist.
7. Focused V42 tests pass.
8. Focused V41 tests still pass.
9. Production-readiness test still returns NOT_PRODUCTION_READY.
10. Patch receipt exists.
11. Updated project zip passes integrity.
12. Final response does not overclaim production readiness.
```

If any item is missing, the patch may still be useful, but it should be marked:

```text
PARTIAL_V42_PATCH
```

not complete.

---

## 26. Failure Modes V42 Must Prevent

The first implementation should explicitly defend against these failure modes.

### 26.1 Apology without artifact repair

The assistant apologizes and continues, but the wrong file remains changed or the correct artifact is never patched.

V42 response:

```text
ARTIFACT_PATCH_OBLIGATION remains REQUIRED until patched or explicitly blocked.
```

### 26.2 Artifact repair without manifest repair

The assistant changes files but does not update manifest/checksum.

V42 response:

```text
MANIFEST_CHECKSUM_OBLIGATION remains REQUIRED.
```

### 26.3 Target drift after correction

The assistant says it understands the live root, then continues modifying the wrong surface.

V42 response:

```text
TARGET_REALIGNMENT failure; repair status returns to REQUIRED or BLOCKED.
```

### 26.4 Overclaim after partial test

The assistant runs focused tests and claims full verification.

V42 response:

```text
SCOPE_NARROWING + AUTHORITY_DOWNGRADE; correction required.
```

### 26.5 Repair receipt as production authority

The assistant claims that because a repair receipt exists, the system is production-ready.

V42 response:

```text
FORBIDDEN_REPRESENTATION_REPAIR or AUTHORITY_DOWNGRADE; production_authority remains false.
```

### 26.6 Visual verification collapse

The assistant treats a screenshot description, DOM read, and UI fix as one completed action.

V42 response:

```text
Separate VISUAL_RECHECK, ARTIFACT_PATCH_OBLIGATION, and evidence requirements.
```

---

## 27. Recommended V42 Handoff Prompt for Implementation Agent

When it is time to patch the live ION project root, the following prompt should be given to the execution agent:

```text
You are operating as the execution agent for ION.

Mission:
Patch the live ION project root with V42_CONVERSATIONAL_RECEIPTS_AND_LIVE_REPAIR as an A3 runtime-inspection branch surface.

Authority:
Do not claim production readiness.
Do not modify unrelated systems except minimal indexes/imports required for discoverability.
Do not override V41 Front-Stage Council Runtime Receipts.
Do not activate unrestricted agents, visual automation, browser control, or daemon authority.

Required inputs:
- Current live ION project root.
- Encyclopedia v2.3 V42 protocol draft.
- Encyclopedia v2.4 V42 project-tree landing blueprint.

Required files to add:
- ION/00_BOOTSTRAP/V42_CONVERSATIONAL_RECEIPTS_AND_LIVE_REPAIR_LOCK.md
- ION/02_architecture/CONVERSATIONAL_RECEIPTS_AND_LIVE_REPAIR_PROTOCOL.md
- ION/03_registry/conversational_repair_receipt.schema.json
- ION/03_registry/conversational_repair_policy.yaml
- ION/04_packages/kernel/conversational_repair_receipt.py
- ION/tests/test_kernel_conversational_repair_receipt.py

Required tests:
- focused V42 test pass
- focused V41 front-stage council receipt test pass
- focused V40 maintained work surface test pass
- production readiness remains NOT_PRODUCTION_READY

Required output:
- updated project zip
- patch receipt
- manifest/checksum updates
- test report
- explicit non-production boundary
```

This handoff prompt should be included in the encyclopedia because ION often operates through external execution agents. The prompt makes the intended implementation path recoverable.

---

## 28. v2.4 Settlement

This section settles the following as encyclopedia design truth:

```yaml
settled:
  - V42 needs a project-tree landing blueprint before implementation
  - V42 first landing should be a runtime-inspection receipt surface, not an automation engine
  - required project files are identified
  - required schema/policy/kernel/test/doc surfaces are specified
  - V42 must extend V41 rather than bypass it
  - artifact-target realignment is a first-class V42 repair behavior
  - user corrections can be authoritative for intent and artifact target while still requiring verification for external facts
  - manifest/checksum repair obligations must be explicit when artifacts are changed
  - the current canvas-to-Markdown correction should become a canonical V42 fixture

not_settled:
  - exact final Python implementation
  - exact final JSON schema after project-tree constraints
  - exact V43 successor name
  - whether the live ION project tree has already been patched with V42
  - full-suite project verification
  - production readiness
```

The next encyclopedia move should be either:

```text
A. draft the V42 candidate project files as appendix text, still inside the encyclopedia packet; or
B. switch to live ION project-root patching once the current project zip is supplied as the target root.
```

For this artifact stream, option A is safer until explicitly moving from encyclopedia evolution to project-root mutation.

---

## 29. Closing Rule

The v2.4 rule is:

```text
A repair protocol is not live until its files, schemas, tests, receipts, manifests, and checksums exist in the correct artifact root.
```

That rule is now part of the encyclopedia’s own behavior. The encyclopedia is not merely describing ION. It is using ION’s logic to keep itself honest.

## Conversational Receipts and Live Repair Candidate Implementation Text

**Authority posture:** encyclopedia appendix / candidate project-file text  
**Production claim:** false  
**Project-root mutation claim:** false  
**Implementation claim:** false

## 1. Purpose of This Appendix

v2.4 settled that the next safe encyclopedia move was to draft the V42 candidate project files as appendix text before mutating the live ION project root. This appendix performs that work.

This is not a project-root patch. It is an implementation-ready design appendix. The candidate files below are written as if they were to be landed into the live ION project tree, but in this artifact they remain encyclopedia text.

The distinction is important:

```text
Encyclopedia appendix text can specify candidate files.
Only a project-root patch can make those files live.
Only tests, receipts, manifests, and checksums in that project root can prove the patch landed.
```

The goal is to give a future implementation agent precise, low-drift material to copy into the correct ION paths.
