## 3. Candidate File: V42 Bootstrap Lock

**Target path:** `ION/00_BOOTSTRAP/V42_CONVERSATIONAL_RECEIPTS_AND_LIVE_REPAIR_LOCK.md`

````markdown
# V42 Conversational Receipts and Live Repair Lock

**Lock ID:** `V42_CONVERSATIONAL_RECEIPTS_AND_LIVE_REPAIR_LOCK`  
**Status:** A3 runtime-inspection branch surface  
**Production authority:** false  
**Global graph canon authority:** false  
**Source-summary rewrite authority:** false  
**Unrestricted agent activation:** false  
**Unrestricted visual/computer-use authority:** false  
**Successor to:** `V41_FRONT_STAGE_COUNCIL_RUNTIME_RECEIPTS_LOCK`  

---

## 1. Purpose

V42 extends V41 Front-Stage Council Runtime Receipts into live conversational repair.

V41 classifies proposed user-facing claims before emission. V42 records what happens when a conversational claim, artifact target, authority level, grounding state, or user intent alignment must be corrected after or during emission.

V42 exists because a governed AI system must not treat correction as a casual apology. Correction is continuity state.

The central rule is:

```text
A correction is not merely an apology. A correction is a continuity event.
```

---

## 2. What V42 Adds

V42 introduces a runtime-inspection receipt for:

```text
user correction
assistant self-correction
artifact-target realignment
claim-class upgrade or downgrade
provisional utterance settlement
repair after wrong authority surface use
visual contradiction repair
manifest/checksum obligation repair
scope narrowing
scope expansion after evidence appears
forbidden representation retraction
```

V42 does not grant production authority. It does not activate unrestricted agents. It does not allow the Persona to claim total ION identity. It does not make repair receipt existence equivalent to correctness.

---

## 3. Required V42 Surfaces

The V42 branch is not considered landed unless the following project-tree surfaces exist:

```text
ION/00_BOOTSTRAP/V42_CONVERSATIONAL_RECEIPTS_AND_LIVE_REPAIR_LOCK.md
ION/02_architecture/CONVERSATIONAL_RECEIPTS_AND_LIVE_REPAIR_PROTOCOL.md
ION/03_registry/conversational_repair_receipt.schema.json
ION/03_registry/conversational_repair_policy.yaml
ION/04_packages/kernel/conversational_repair_receipt.py
ION/tests/test_kernel_conversational_repair_receipt.py
```

The V42 branch is not considered verified unless focused tests for V42, V41, V40, and production readiness pass under the live project root.

---

## 4. Inheritance

V42 inherits from:

```text
V40 Maintained Work Surface and Persona-System Canon
V41 Front-Stage Council Runtime Receipts
Representational Integrity Protocol
Live Persona Latency and Provisional Utterance Protocol
Expressive Telemetry and Affect Integrity Protocol
Visual Perception and Interaction Agent Protocol
Production Readiness Gap Register
```

V42 must not bypass V41. A repair receipt is downstream of front-stage council claim handling, not a replacement for it.

---

## 5. Forbidden Collapses

V42 forbids the following collapses:

```text
chat correction == artifact correction
apology == repair receipt
repair receipt == production authority
user frustration == factual proof
visual observation == verified source truth
manifest update == checksum verification
claim downgrade == task completion
```

Each may be related to repair, but each remains a distinct state.

---

## 6. Next Branch

The next branch after V42 should not be named here unless the project root later ratifies a successor. Candidate successor themes include:

```text
repair-aware artifact regeneration
conversation-to-project patch receipts
front-stage council repair dashboards
production-gate namespace reconciliation
```

No successor is activated by this lock.
````

---

## 4. Candidate File: V42 Protocol

**Target path:** `ION/02_architecture/CONVERSATIONAL_RECEIPTS_AND_LIVE_REPAIR_PROTOCOL.md`

````markdown
# Conversational Receipts and Live Repair Protocol

**Protocol ID:** `CONVERSATIONAL_RECEIPTS_AND_LIVE_REPAIR_PROTOCOL`  
**Branch:** `V42_CONVERSATIONAL_RECEIPTS_AND_LIVE_REPAIR`  
**Status:** A3 runtime-inspection protocol  
**Production authority:** false  
**Depends on:** `FRONT_STAGE_COUNCIL_RUNTIME_RECEIPT_PROTOCOL`  

---

## 1. Definition

Conversational repair is the governed correction of a claim, artifact target, scope, authority level, grounding state, user-intent interpretation, or emitted representation during live AI-mediated work.

A repair receipt is the runtime object that records:

```text
what was wrong or misaligned;
who or what triggered the correction;
which prior claim or action is affected;
how the claim class moved;
what artifact or state must be patched;
whether user-facing repair is required;
whether downstream receipts/manifests/checksums must change;
whether the repair is complete, partial, blocked, or only acknowledged.
```

---

## 2. Why This Protocol Exists

ION’s front-stage council prevents many overclaims before emission, but real collaboration also requires post-emission correction. The user may clarify that the target was wrong. A file may have been updated in the wrong place. A claim may be discovered to rely on weaker evidence than first believed. A visual observation may contradict an implementation claim. A test may pass locally but the artifact manifest may not include the changed file.

A normal assistant often handles this with apology text. ION must handle it as state.

The core rule is:

```text
Chat correction does not equal artifact correction.
```

Repair must be grounded, typed, and followed through to the affected artifact or claim boundary.

---

## 3. Relationship to V41

V41 classifies claims before emission:

```text
claim text
→ claim class
→ Persona state
→ Relay grounding state
→ Steward/VZ verdict
→ risk level
→ emission permission
→ visibility level
→ repair obligation
```

V42 records what happens when that lane requires correction:

```text
prior claim or action
→ repair trigger
→ repair class
→ claim-class movement
→ artifact obligation
→ user-facing repair permission
→ completion status
→ receipt
```

V42 is downstream from V41 and must not bypass it.

---

## 4. Repair Classes

V42 recognizes the following repair classes:

```text
ARTIFACT_TARGET_REALIGNMENT
CLAIM_CLASS_DOWNGRADE
CLAIM_CLASS_UPGRADE
PROVISIONAL_SETTLEMENT
SCOPE_NARROWING
SCOPE_EXPANSION
AUTHORITY_DOWNGRADE
AUTHORITY_UPGRADE
GROUNDING_REPAIR
MANIFEST_REPAIR
CHECKSUM_REPAIR
VISUAL_RECHECK
USER_INTENT_REBINDING
FORBIDDEN_REPRESENTATION_RETRACTION
TASK_STATE_REOPEN
TASK_STATE_CLOSEOUT
```

### 4.1 Artifact-target realignment

Used when the assistant worked in or referenced the wrong target surface.

Example:

```text
wrong target: canvas side document
correct target: Markdown file inside encyclopedia packet
repair: stop canvas writes, migrate useful content into correct MD, regenerate zip, update manifest/checksums
```

### 4.2 Claim-class downgrade

Used when a claim was emitted with stronger authority than evidence supports.

Example:

```text
C0 direct verified state -> C2 proposal
```

### 4.3 Claim-class upgrade

Used when additional evidence supports a stronger claim. Upgrades require evidence and must not be driven by user preference alone.

### 4.4 Provisional settlement

Used when an L0/L1 provisional utterance must be checked, ratified, narrowed, or retracted.

### 4.5 Visual recheck

Used when rendered behavior, screenshot evidence, DOM state, or UI behavior contradicts an implementation or completion claim.

---

## 5. Repair Trigger Classes

Allowed trigger classes:

```text
USER_CORRECTION
ASSISTANT_SELF_DETECTION
TEST_FAILURE
ARTIFACT_MISSING
WRONG_ARTIFACT_ROOT
MANIFEST_MISMATCH
CHECKSUM_MISMATCH
VISUAL_CONTRADICTION
POLICY_CONTRADICTION
AUTHORITY_CONTRADICTION
GROUNDING_GAP
POST_ACTION_EVIDENCE_GAP
```

User correction is authoritative for user intent, requested target, dissatisfaction, and conversation-scope rebinding. User correction is not automatically authoritative for external facts, file contents, test outcomes, or production readiness.

---

## 6. Repair Status Values

Repair receipts use the following statuses:

```text
ACKNOWLEDGED
IN_PROGRESS
PATCHED_IN_CHAT_ONLY
PATCHED_IN_ARTIFACT
PATCHED_IN_PROJECT_ROOT
VERIFIED
PARTIAL
BLOCKED
SUPERSEDED
RETRACTED
```

Important distinction:

```text
PATCHED_IN_CHAT_ONLY is not equivalent to PATCHED_IN_ARTIFACT.
PATCHED_IN_ARTIFACT is not equivalent to PATCHED_IN_PROJECT_ROOT.
PATCHED_IN_PROJECT_ROOT is not equivalent to PRODUCTION_READY.
```

---

## 7. Claim-Class Movement Ledger

Each repair receipt may include a claim-class movement ledger:

```yaml
claim_class_before: C0 | C1 | C2 | C3 | C4 | C5 | unknown
claim_class_after: C0 | C1 | C2 | C3 | C4 | C5 | unchanged
movement_reason: <why the movement occurred>
evidence_added:
  - <evidence>
evidence_removed_or_invalidated:
  - <evidence>
user_visible_repair_required: true | false
```

Claim-class movement must never be hidden when the original claim was high-impact.

---

## 8. Artifact Obligation Ledger

When repair affects an artifact, the receipt must record artifact obligations:

```yaml
affected_artifacts:
  - path: <path>
    obligation: add | modify | remove | regenerate | checksum | manifest | verify | none
    status: pending | complete | blocked
```

If an artifact zip is changed, V42 expects manifest/checksum regeneration unless the artifact format has no manifest/checksum convention.

---

## 9. Visibility Levels

V42 inherits V41 visibility levels and adds repair-specific interpretation:

```text
QUIET — no user-facing repair needed; internal low-risk adjustment only
EXPANDABLE — user can inspect repair receipt if desired
MANDATORY — repair must be stated to user
BLOCKING — work must stop or change target before continuing
```

A wrong artifact root is normally `BLOCKING` until the target is corrected.

---

## 10. State Machine

The minimal V42 state machine:

```text
NO_REPAIR_REQUIRED
→ REPAIR_TRIGGERED
→ REPAIR_CLASSIFIED
→ OBLIGATIONS_IDENTIFIED
→ PATCH_ATTEMPTED
→ EVIDENCE_RECHECKED
→ REPAIR_VERIFIED | REPAIR_PARTIAL | REPAIR_BLOCKED | REPAIR_SUPERSEDED
```

A repair cannot move to `REPAIR_VERIFIED` unless the evidence required by the repair class exists.

---

## 11. Forbidden Representational Repairs

If the assistant implies false identity, hidden omniscience, total ION embodiment, independent completion of specialist work, or production readiness without evidence, V42 must classify the repair as:

```text
FORBIDDEN_REPRESENTATION_RETRACTION
```

The repair must include:

```text
retraction
correct representation
affected claim
visibility level
whether future guard update is required
```

---

## 12. Integration With Visual Perception and Interaction Agent

Visual contradiction repairs occur when visual/rendered evidence disagrees with a claim.

Examples:

```text
assistant says UI is fixed, screenshot shows overflow
assistant says DOM was changed, only screenshot was inspected
assistant claims visual verification, but no before/after receipt exists
```

V42 must separate:

```text
visual observation
visual diagnosis
patch request
artifact patch
post-patch visual verify
visual repair receipt
```

---

## 13. Completion Standard

A V42 repair is complete only when:

```text
repair trigger is recorded;
repair class is assigned;
affected claim/artifact is identified;
claim-class movement is recorded if applicable;
artifact obligations are satisfied or explicitly blocked;
user-facing visibility requirement is satisfied;
required receipts/manifests/checksums/tests are updated when applicable;
final status is not merely conversational unless the repair is only conversational.
```

---

## 14. Non-Production Boundary

This protocol is a runtime-inspection and repair-governance surface. It does not grant production readiness. It does not make repaired claims true by default. It does not authorize hidden mutation or unrestricted automation.
````

---

````yaml
version: V42_CONVERSATIONAL_RECEIPTS_AND_LIVE_REPAIR
status: A3_runtime_inspection_policy
production_authority: false
inherits_from:
  - V41_FRONT_STAGE_COUNCIL_RUNTIME_RECEIPTS
  - V40_MAINTAINED_WORK_SURFACE_AND_PERSONA_SYSTEM_CANON

repair_statuses:
  - ACKNOWLEDGED
  - IN_PROGRESS
  - PATCHED_IN_CHAT_ONLY
  - PATCHED_IN_ARTIFACT
  - PATCHED_IN_PROJECT_ROOT
  - VERIFIED
  - PARTIAL
  - BLOCKED
  - SUPERSEDED
  - RETRACTED

repair_classes:
  - ARTIFACT_TARGET_REALIGNMENT
  - CLAIM_CLASS_DOWNGRADE
  - CLAIM_CLASS_UPGRADE
  - PROVISIONAL_SETTLEMENT
  - SCOPE_NARROWING
  - SCOPE_EXPANSION
  - AUTHORITY_DOWNGRADE
  - AUTHORITY_UPGRADE
  - GROUNDING_REPAIR
  - MANIFEST_REPAIR
  - CHECKSUM_REPAIR
  - VISUAL_RECHECK
  - USER_INTENT_REBINDING
  - FORBIDDEN_REPRESENTATION_RETRACTION
  - TASK_STATE_REOPEN
  - TASK_STATE_CLOSEOUT

trigger_classes:
  - USER_CORRECTION
  - ASSISTANT_SELF_DETECTION
  - TEST_FAILURE
  - ARTIFACT_MISSING
  - WRONG_ARTIFACT_ROOT
  - MANIFEST_MISMATCH
  - CHECKSUM_MISMATCH
  - VISUAL_CONTRADICTION
  - POLICY_CONTRADICTION
  - AUTHORITY_CONTRADICTION
  - GROUNDING_GAP
  - POST_ACTION_EVIDENCE_GAP

visibility_levels:
  - QUIET
  - EXPANDABLE
  - MANDATORY
  - BLOCKING

rules:
  chat_correction_is_not_artifact_correction: true
  repair_receipt_is_not_production_authority: true
  wrong_artifact_root_is_blocking: true
  artifact_zip_change_requires_manifest_or_checksum_review: true
  high_impact_claim_movement_requires_visibility: true
  user_correction_authoritative_for_intent: true
  user_correction_not_automatic_external_fact_proof: true
  visual_claim_repair_requires_visual_evidence_boundary: true

status_order:
  acknowledged_only:
    allows_completion_claim: false
  patched_in_chat_only:
    allows_artifact_claim: false
  patched_in_artifact:
    allows_project_root_claim: false
  patched_in_project_root:
    allows_production_claim: false
  verified:
    allows_production_claim: false

blocking_repair_classes:
  - ARTIFACT_TARGET_REALIGNMENT
  - FORBIDDEN_REPRESENTATION_RETRACTION
  - CHECKSUM_REPAIR
  - MANIFEST_REPAIR

never_provisional:
  - production_authority
  - destructive_action
  - credential_sensitive_action
  - legal_medical_financial_high_stakes_guidance
  - identity_or_personhood_claim
  - file_or_test_proof_claim
````

## 7. Candidate File: Kernel Module

**Target path:** `ION/04_packages/kernel/conversational_repair_receipt.py`

````python
"""ION V42 conversational repair receipt runtime-inspection surface.

This module is intentionally small and deterministic. It records repair receipts
for conversational correction, artifact-target realignment, claim-class movement,
and live repair obligations. It does not grant production authority.
"""

from __future__ import annotations

from dataclasses import dataclass, field, asdict
from datetime import datetime, timezone
from enum import Enum
from typing import Iterable, Mapping, Any
from uuid import uuid4


VERSION = "V42_CONVERSATIONAL_RECEIPTS_AND_LIVE_REPAIR"
PRODUCTION_AUTHORITY = False


class RepairStatus(str, Enum):
    ACKNOWLEDGED = "ACKNOWLEDGED"
    IN_PROGRESS = "IN_PROGRESS"
    PATCHED_IN_CHAT_ONLY = "PATCHED_IN_CHAT_ONLY"
    PATCHED_IN_ARTIFACT = "PATCHED_IN_ARTIFACT"
    PATCHED_IN_PROJECT_ROOT = "PATCHED_IN_PROJECT_ROOT"
    VERIFIED = "VERIFIED"
    PARTIAL = "PARTIAL"
    BLOCKED = "BLOCKED"
    SUPERSEDED = "SUPERSEDED"
    RETRACTED = "RETRACTED"


class RepairClass(str, Enum):
    ARTIFACT_TARGET_REALIGNMENT = "ARTIFACT_TARGET_REALIGNMENT"
    CLAIM_CLASS_DOWNGRADE = "CLAIM_CLASS_DOWNGRADE"
    CLAIM_CLASS_UPGRADE = "CLAIM_CLASS_UPGRADE"
    PROVISIONAL_SETTLEMENT = "PROVISIONAL_SETTLEMENT"
    SCOPE_NARROWING = "SCOPE_NARROWING"
    SCOPE_EXPANSION = "SCOPE_EXPANSION"
    AUTHORITY_DOWNGRADE = "AUTHORITY_DOWNGRADE"
    AUTHORITY_UPGRADE = "AUTHORITY_UPGRADE"
    GROUNDING_REPAIR = "GROUNDING_REPAIR"
    MANIFEST_REPAIR = "MANIFEST_REPAIR"
    CHECKSUM_REPAIR = "CHECKSUM_REPAIR"
    VISUAL_RECHECK = "VISUAL_RECHECK"
    USER_INTENT_REBINDING = "USER_INTENT_REBINDING"
    FORBIDDEN_REPRESENTATION_RETRACTION = "FORBIDDEN_REPRESENTATION_RETRACTION"
    TASK_STATE_REOPEN = "TASK_STATE_REOPEN"
    TASK_STATE_CLOSEOUT = "TASK_STATE_CLOSEOUT"


class TriggerClass(str, Enum):
    USER_CORRECTION = "USER_CORRECTION"
    ASSISTANT_SELF_DETECTION = "ASSISTANT_SELF_DETECTION"
    TEST_FAILURE = "TEST_FAILURE"
    ARTIFACT_MISSING = "ARTIFACT_MISSING"
    WRONG_ARTIFACT_ROOT = "WRONG_ARTIFACT_ROOT"
    MANIFEST_MISMATCH = "MANIFEST_MISMATCH"
    CHECKSUM_MISMATCH = "CHECKSUM_MISMATCH"
    VISUAL_CONTRADICTION = "VISUAL_CONTRADICTION"
    POLICY_CONTRADICTION = "POLICY_CONTRADICTION"
    AUTHORITY_CONTRADICTION = "AUTHORITY_CONTRADICTION"
    GROUNDING_GAP = "GROUNDING_GAP"
    POST_ACTION_EVIDENCE_GAP = "POST_ACTION_EVIDENCE_GAP"


class VisibilityLevel(str, Enum):
    QUIET = "QUIET"
    EXPANDABLE = "EXPANDABLE"
    MANDATORY = "MANDATORY"
    BLOCKING = "BLOCKING"


VALID_CLAIM_CLASSES = {"C0", "C1", "C2", "C3", "C4", "C5", "unknown", "unchanged"}


@dataclass(frozen=True)
class ArtifactObligation:
    path: str
    obligation: str
    status: str = "pending"

    def validate(self) -> None:
        allowed_obligations = {"add", "modify", "remove", "regenerate", "checksum", "manifest", "verify", "none"}
        allowed_statuses = {"pending", "complete", "blocked"}
        if not self.path:
            raise ValueError("artifact obligation path is required")
        if self.obligation not in allowed_obligations:
            raise ValueError(f"invalid artifact obligation: {self.obligation}")
        if self.status not in allowed_statuses:
            raise ValueError(f"invalid artifact obligation status: {self.status}")


@dataclass(frozen=True)
class ConversationalRepairReceipt:
    receipt_id: str
    repair_status: RepairStatus
    repair_classes: tuple[RepairClass, ...]
    trigger_class: TriggerClass
    prior_claim_or_action: str
    corrected_claim_or_action: str = ""
    claim_class_before: str = "unknown"
    claim_class_after: str = "unchanged"
    movement_reason: str = ""
    affected_artifacts: tuple[ArtifactObligation, ...] = field(default_factory=tuple)
    evidence_added: tuple[str, ...] = field(default_factory=tuple)
    evidence_invalidated: tuple[str, ...] = field(default_factory=tuple)
    visibility_level: VisibilityLevel = VisibilityLevel.EXPANDABLE
    user_visible_repair_required: bool = False
    repair_obligations: tuple[str, ...] = field(default_factory=tuple)
    repair_notes: str = ""
    created_at: str = field(default_factory=lambda: datetime.now(timezone.utc).isoformat())
    version: str = VERSION
    production_authority: bool = PRODUCTION_AUTHORITY

    def validate(self) -> None:
        if self.version != VERSION:
            raise ValueError(f"invalid version: {self.version}")
        if self.production_authority is not False:
            raise ValueError("V42 repair receipts cannot grant production authority")
        if not self.receipt_id:
            raise ValueError("receipt_id is required")
        if not self.prior_claim_or_action:
            raise ValueError("prior_claim_or_action is required")
        if not self.repair_classes:
            raise ValueError("at least one repair class is required")
        if self.claim_class_before not in VALID_CLAIM_CLASSES:
            raise ValueError(f"invalid claim_class_before: {self.claim_class_before}")
        if self.claim_class_after not in VALID_CLAIM_CLASSES:
            raise ValueError(f"invalid claim_class_after: {self.claim_class_after}")
        for obligation in self.affected_artifacts:
            obligation.validate()
        if self._is_wrong_artifact_root() and self.visibility_level != VisibilityLevel.BLOCKING:
            raise ValueError("wrong artifact root repairs require BLOCKING visibility")
        if self._is_high_impact_claim_movement() and not self.user_visible_repair_required:
            raise ValueError("high-impact claim movement requires user-visible repair")

    def _is_wrong_artifact_root(self) -> bool:
        return (
            self.trigger_class == TriggerClass.WRONG_ARTIFACT_ROOT
            or RepairClass.ARTIFACT_TARGET_REALIGNMENT in self.repair_classes
        )

    def _is_high_impact_claim_movement(self) -> bool:
        before = self.claim_class_before
        after = self.claim_class_after
        if before in {"C0", "C1"} and after in {"C2", "C3", "C4", "C5"}:
            return True
        if RepairClass.FORBIDDEN_REPRESENTATION_RETRACTION in self.repair_classes:
            return True
        return False

    def as_dict(self) -> dict[str, Any]:
        self.validate()
        data = asdict(self)
        data["repair_status"] = self.repair_status.value
        data["repair_classes"] = [item.value for item in self.repair_classes]
        data["trigger_class"] = self.trigger_class.value
        data["visibility_level"] = self.visibility_level.value
        return data


def _coerce_repair_classes(values: Iterable[str | RepairClass]) -> tuple[RepairClass, ...]:
    coerced = tuple(value if isinstance(value, RepairClass) else RepairClass(value) for value in values)
    if not coerced:
        raise ValueError("repair_classes cannot be empty")
    return coerced


def _coerce_artifact_obligations(values: Iterable[Mapping[str, str]] | None) -> tuple[ArtifactObligation, ...]:
    if not values:
        return tuple()
    return tuple(ArtifactObligation(**dict(value)) for value in values)


def create_repair_receipt(
    *,
    repair_status: str | RepairStatus,
    repair_classes: Iterable[str | RepairClass],
    trigger_class: str | TriggerClass,
    prior_claim_or_action: str,
    corrected_claim_or_action: str = "",
    claim_class_before: str = "unknown",
    claim_class_after: str = "unchanged",
    movement_reason: str = "",
    affected_artifacts: Iterable[Mapping[str, str]] | None = None,
    evidence_added: Iterable[str] = (),
    evidence_invalidated: Iterable[str] = (),
    visibility_level: str | VisibilityLevel = VisibilityLevel.EXPANDABLE,
    user_visible_repair_required: bool = False,
    repair_obligations: Iterable[str] = (),
    repair_notes: str = "",
    receipt_id: str | None = None,
) -> ConversationalRepairReceipt:
    """Create and validate a V42 conversational repair receipt."""

    receipt = ConversationalRepairReceipt(
        receipt_id=receipt_id or f"v42-repair-{uuid4().hex}",
        repair_status=repair_status if isinstance(repair_status, RepairStatus) else RepairStatus(repair_status),
        repair_classes=_coerce_repair_classes(repair_classes),
        trigger_class=trigger_class if isinstance(trigger_class, TriggerClass) else TriggerClass(trigger_class),
        prior_claim_or_action=prior_claim_or_action,
        corrected_claim_or_action=corrected_claim_or_action,
        claim_class_before=claim_class_before,
        claim_class_after=claim_class_after,
        movement_reason=movement_reason,
        affected_artifacts=_coerce_artifact_obligations(affected_artifacts),
        evidence_added=tuple(evidence_added),
        evidence_invalidated=tuple(evidence_invalidated),
        visibility_level=visibility_level if isinstance(visibility_level, VisibilityLevel) else VisibilityLevel(visibility_level),
        user_visible_repair_required=bool(user_visible_repair_required),
        repair_obligations=tuple(repair_obligations),
        repair_notes=repair_notes,
    )
    receipt.validate()
    return receipt


def report_v42_status() -> dict[str, Any]:
    """Return a deterministic V42 runtime-inspection status report."""

    return {
        "version": VERSION,
        "verdict": "VALID_V42_CONVERSATIONAL_RECEIPTS_AND_LIVE_REPAIR_SURFACE",
        "production_authority": PRODUCTION_AUTHORITY,
        "depends_on": [
            "V41_FRONT_STAGE_COUNCIL_RUNTIME_RECEIPTS",
            "V40_MAINTAINED_WORK_SURFACE_AND_PERSONA_SYSTEM_CANON",
        ],
        "repair_classes": [item.value for item in RepairClass],
        "trigger_classes": [item.value for item in TriggerClass],
        "repair_statuses": [item.value for item in RepairStatus],
        "visibility_levels": [item.value for item in VisibilityLevel],
        "core_rules": {
            "chat_correction_is_not_artifact_correction": True,
            "repair_receipt_is_not_production_authority": True,
            "wrong_artifact_root_is_blocking": True,
        },
    }
````

---

## 8. Candidate File: Unit Tests

**Target path:** `ION/tests/test_kernel_conversational_repair_receipt.py`

````python
import unittest

from kernel.conversational_repair_receipt import (
    PRODUCTION_AUTHORITY,
    VERSION,
    RepairClass,
    RepairStatus,
    TriggerClass,
    VisibilityLevel,
    create_repair_receipt,
    report_v42_status,
)


class ConversationalRepairReceiptTests(unittest.TestCase):
    def test_status_report_preserves_non_production_authority(self):
        report = report_v42_status()
        self.assertEqual(report["version"], VERSION)
        self.assertFalse(report["production_authority"])
        self.assertFalse(PRODUCTION_AUTHORITY)
        self.assertIn("ARTIFACT_TARGET_REALIGNMENT", report["repair_classes"])
        self.assertIn("WRONG_ARTIFACT_ROOT", report["trigger_classes"])

    def test_basic_user_correction_receipt(self):
        receipt = create_repair_receipt(
            repair_status=RepairStatus.ACKNOWLEDGED,
            repair_classes=[RepairClass.USER_INTENT_REBINDING],
            trigger_class=TriggerClass.USER_CORRECTION,
            prior_claim_or_action="Assistant treated canvas as target root.",
            corrected_claim_or_action="Use Markdown encyclopedia packet as target root.",
            visibility_level=VisibilityLevel.MANDATORY,
            user_visible_repair_required=True,
        )
        data = receipt.as_dict()
        self.assertEqual(data["version"], VERSION)
        self.assertEqual(data["repair_status"], "ACKNOWLEDGED")
        self.assertEqual(data["trigger_class"], "USER_CORRECTION")
        self.assertFalse(data["production_authority"])

    def test_wrong_artifact_root_requires_blocking_visibility(self):
        with self.assertRaises(ValueError):
            create_repair_receipt(
                repair_status="IN_PROGRESS",
                repair_classes=["ARTIFACT_TARGET_REALIGNMENT"],
                trigger_class="WRONG_ARTIFACT_ROOT",
                prior_claim_or_action="Wrote to the wrong target surface.",
                visibility_level="MANDATORY",
                user_visible_repair_required=True,
            )

    def test_wrong_artifact_root_receipt_with_artifact_obligation(self):
        receipt = create_repair_receipt(
            repair_status="PATCHED_IN_ARTIFACT",
            repair_classes=["ARTIFACT_TARGET_REALIGNMENT", "MANIFEST_REPAIR", "CHECKSUM_REPAIR"],
            trigger_class="WRONG_ARTIFACT_ROOT",
            prior_claim_or_action="Used side canvas as authority surface.",
            corrected_claim_or_action="Updated encyclopedia Markdown packet directly.",
            affected_artifacts=[
                {"path": "ION_Production_Encyclopedia_v2_5_*.zip", "obligation": "regenerate", "status": "complete"},
                {"path": "ION_Production_Encyclopedia_v2_5_CHECKSUMS.sha256", "obligation": "checksum", "status": "complete"},
                {"path": "ION_Production_Encyclopedia_v2_5_CONSOLIDATED_MANIFEST.json", "obligation": "manifest", "status": "complete"},
            ],
            visibility_level="BLOCKING",
            user_visible_repair_required=True,
        )
        data = receipt.as_dict()
        self.assertEqual(data["repair_status"], "PATCHED_IN_ARTIFACT")
        self.assertEqual(len(data["affected_artifacts"]), 3)

    def test_high_impact_claim_downgrade_requires_user_visible_repair(self):
        with self.assertRaises(ValueError):
            create_repair_receipt(
                repair_status="ACKNOWLEDGED",
                repair_classes=["CLAIM_CLASS_DOWNGRADE"],
                trigger_class="ASSISTANT_SELF_DETECTION",
                prior_claim_or_action="Claimed full-suite verification.",
                corrected_claim_or_action="Only focused tests were run.",
                claim_class_before="C0",
                claim_class_after="C2",
                movement_reason="Evidence did not support the stronger claim.",
                visibility_level="EXPANDABLE",
                user_visible_repair_required=False,
            )

    def test_high_impact_claim_downgrade_allowed_when_visible(self):
        receipt = create_repair_receipt(
            repair_status="VERIFIED",
            repair_classes=["CLAIM_CLASS_DOWNGRADE"],
            trigger_class="ASSISTANT_SELF_DETECTION",
            prior_claim_or_action="Claimed full-suite verification.",
            corrected_claim_or_action="Only focused tests were run.",
            claim_class_before="C0",
            claim_class_after="C2",
            movement_reason="Evidence did not support the stronger claim.",
            visibility_level="MANDATORY",
            user_visible_repair_required=True,
            evidence_added=["Focused unittest output"],
            evidence_invalidated=["Full pytest claim"],
        )
        self.assertEqual(receipt.as_dict()["claim_class_after"], "C2")

    def test_repair_receipt_never_grants_production_authority(self):
        receipt = create_repair_receipt(
            repair_status="VERIFIED",
            repair_classes=["TASK_STATE_CLOSEOUT"],
            trigger_class="ASSISTANT_SELF_DETECTION",
            prior_claim_or_action="Repair task completed.",
            corrected_claim_or_action="Repair task completed within V42 non-production boundary.",
            visibility_level="EXPANDABLE",
        )
        self.assertFalse(receipt.as_dict()["production_authority"])


if __name__ == "__main__":
    unittest.main()
````

---

## 9. Minimal Index/Import Guidance

If the live project uses package-level exports, add only the minimal import surface needed for discoverability. Do not make V42 the default runtime entrypoint.

Candidate addition to `ION/04_packages/kernel/__init__.py`, only if such exports are already used:

````python
# V42 conversational repair receipt surface
# Non-production runtime-inspection helper.
````

No production launcher should be added by this patch.

---

## 10. Required Focused Verification Command

The implementation agent should run a focused test command equivalent to:

```bash
PYTHONPATH=ION/04_packages python -S -m unittest \
  ION.tests.test_kernel_conversational_repair_receipt \
  ION.tests.test_kernel_front_stage_council_receipt \
  ION.tests.test_kernel_maintained_work_surface \
  ION.tests.test_kernel_production_readiness -v
```

Expected focused result after successful V42 landing:

```text
V42 tests pass.
V41 front-stage council receipt tests still pass.
V40 maintained work surface tests still pass.
Production readiness still returns NOT_PRODUCTION_READY.
```

The implementation agent must not claim full-suite verification unless the full suite actually runs and passes.

---

## 11. Candidate V42 Landing Receipt Shape

A future project-root patch should produce a receipt shaped like:

```yaml
receipt_id: v42-conversational-repair-project-root-landing-<date>
receipt_class: project_root_patch_receipt
branch: V42_CONVERSATIONAL_RECEIPTS_AND_LIVE_REPAIR
production_authority: false
files_added:
  - ION/00_BOOTSTRAP/V42_CONVERSATIONAL_RECEIPTS_AND_LIVE_REPAIR_LOCK.md
  - ION/02_architecture/CONVERSATIONAL_RECEIPTS_AND_LIVE_REPAIR_PROTOCOL.md
  - ION/03_registry/conversational_repair_receipt.schema.json
  - ION/03_registry/conversational_repair_policy.yaml
  - ION/04_packages/kernel/conversational_repair_receipt.py
  - ION/tests/test_kernel_conversational_repair_receipt.py
focused_tests:
  v42: pass | fail | not_run
  v41: pass | fail | not_run
  v40: pass | fail | not_run
  production_readiness: pass | fail | not_run
production_readiness_verdict: NOT_PRODUCTION_READY
claim_boundary:
  - V42 landed as A3 runtime-inspection surface only
  - no production authority granted
  - no unrestricted automation activated
  - no source-summary rewrite authority granted
```

---

## 12. Failure Modes This Appendix Prevents

This appendix is designed to prevent these failures:

```text
1. Implementing V42 from memory instead of from a stable candidate file set.
2. Landing only a protocol document without schema, policy, kernel, and tests.
3. Treating a chat apology as an artifact repair.
4. Treating a repair receipt as production authority.
5. Forgetting V41/V40 regression checks.
6. Patching the wrong root again.
7. Updating a zip without checksum/manifest repair.
8. Claiming full-suite verification from focused tests.
9. Letting user correction automatically become external-fact truth.
10. Collapsing visual recheck into source-code proof.
```

---

## 13. v2.5 Settlement

This appendix settles:

```yaml
settled:
  - V42 candidate project files have now been drafted as encyclopedia appendix text
  - the candidate file set includes lock, protocol, schema, policy, kernel module, and tests
  - candidate runtime behavior preserves production_authority=false
  - wrong artifact root repairs require blocking visibility
  - high-impact claim downgrades require user-visible repair
  - repair receipt existence cannot grant production authority
  - focused verification command is specified

not_settled:
  - live ION project-root V42 implementation
  - exact compatibility with every existing project import/index convention
  - full-suite project test result
  - production readiness
  - successor branch naming after V42
```

The next encyclopedia move should be a production-gate namespace reconciliation chapter, because the live V34–V42 branch numbering now conflicts with older production-gate roadmap numbering. That chapter should distinguish:

```text
live branch lineage numbers
production-gate identifiers
demo/prototype milestone numbers
documentation artifact version numbers
```

Without that distinction, future agents may confuse `V36_SELF_SURFACE_DRIFT_GATE` with the older `V36_GLOBAL_GRAPH_CANON` production-gate concept.
